### Round 2: Brazilian Grand Prix
*Date: 1975-01-26*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 6: Belgian Grand Prix
*Date: 1975-05-25*

### Round 11: German Grand Prix
